## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x2AB4 [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()
  1: 0x2AB5 [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x7923)
  2: 0x2AB8 [0x46] CAMERA_CONTROL: Disable user control
  3: 0x2ABA [0x38] SET_CLIENT_EVENT_MODE(mode=19*)
  4: 0x2ABD [0x4E] SET_ENTITY_HIDE_FLAG: Show LocalPlayer
```
